        }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;

        }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<span class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





the use-after-free is caused by the occlusionQuery (vk::Query) object. [1]



<span class="line"><!---->the use-after-free is caused by the occlusionQuery (vk::Query) object. [1]<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





void DrawCall::setup()



<span class="line"><!---->void DrawCall::setup()<!----></span>



<br>





{



<span class="line"><!---->{<!----></span>



<br>





	if(occlusionQuery != nullptr)



<span class="line"><!---->	if(occlusionQuery != nullptr)<!----></span>



<br>





	{



<span class="line"><!---->	{<!----></span>



<br>





		occlusionQuery->start();



<span class="line"><!---->		occlusionQuery-&gt;start();<!----></span>



<br>





	}



<span class="line"><!---->	}<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The query object is allocated by gl.clear([2]) and set by gl.beginQuery as a member variable of the Renderer.



<span class="line"><!---->The query object is allocated by gl.clear([2]) and set by gl.beginQuery as a member variable of the Renderer.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>





void Renderer::addQuery(vk::Query *query)



<span class="line"><!---->void Renderer::addQuery(vk::Query *query)<!----></span>



<br>





{



<span class="line"><!---->{<!----></span>



<br>





	ASSERT(query->getType() == VK_QUERY_TYPE_OCCLUSION);



<span class="line"><!---->	ASSERT(query-&gt;getType() == VK_QUERY_TYPE_OCCLUSION);<!----></span>



<br>





	ASSERT(!occlusionQuery);



<span class="line"><!---->	ASSERT(!occlusionQuery);<!----></span>



<br>





	occlusionQuery = query;



<span class="line"><!---->	occlusionQuery = query;<!----></span>



<br>





}



<span class="line"><!---->}<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This query object is freed by vkDestroyQueryPool([4]), which seems to be caused by location.href [5]



<span class="line"><!---->This query object is freed by vkDestroyQueryPool([4]), which seems to be caused by location.href [5]<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





However, during the Context::onDestroy process, no one called Renderer::removeQuery, and `occlusionQuery` still has a reference to the freed pointer [6]



<span class="line"><!---->However, during the Context::onDestroy process, no one called Renderer::removeQuery, and `occlusionQuery` still has a reference to the freed pointer [6]<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I think the patch should reset the occlusionQuery pointer via removeQuery in the destroy process.



<span class="line"><!---->I think the patch should reset the occlusionQuery pointer via removeQuery in the destroy process.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

The query oject in the backtrace is a renderPass query (since it is allocated from  rx::QueryVk::onRenderPassStart). 



<span class="line"><!---->The query oject in the backtrace is a renderPass query (since it is allocated from  rx::QueryVk::onRenderPassStart). <!----></span>



<br>





renderPass query's queue serial is set when endQuery is called, (from QueryHelper::endRenderPassQuery()) 



<span class="line"><!---->renderPass query's queue serial is set when endQuery is called, (from QueryHelper::endRenderPassQuery()) <!----></span>



<br>





renderPass query's mUse is merged into  DynamicallyGrowingPool<Pool>'s mUse when query is freed. (From DynamicallyGrowingPool<Pool>::onEntryFreed())



<span class="line"><!---->renderPass query's mUse is merged into  DynamicallyGrowingPool&lt;Pool&gt;'s mUse when query is freed. (From DynamicallyGrowingPool&lt;Pool&gt;::onEntryFreed())<!----></span>



<br>





So the ResourceUse tracking appears okay, even though a bit confusing.



<span class="line"><!---->So the ResourceUse tracking appears okay, even though a bit confusing.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The other big question is the context is already destroyed, but the query is still actively used by swiftshader. This indicates some how renderer->finish() call is not actually finishing. Note that the query pool is per context. When we destroy context, we make sure all commands on the context has been finished. If there is a bug in that code path, then you will run into this. But looking at the implementation, I am also not seeing obvious bug here.



<span class="line"><!---->The other big question is the context is already destroyed, but the query is still actively used by swiftshader. This indicates some how renderer-&gt;finish() call is not actually finishing. Note that the query pool is per context. When we destroy context, we make sure all commands on the context has been finished. If there is a bug in that code path, then you will run into this. But looking at the implementation, I am also not seeing obvious bug here.<!----></span>

Vulkan: Don't close render pass if rebind to same fbo



<span class="line"><!---->Vulkan: Don't close render pass if rebind to same fbo<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In the Vulkan backend, the render pass can occasionally (and



<span class="line"><!---->In the Vulkan backend, the render pass can occasionally (and<!----></span>



<br>





transiently) be in a state of "open but inactive".  This is when the



<span class="line"><!---->transiently) be in a state of "open but inactive".  This is when the<!----></span>



<br>





render pass is closed, but has the potential for future modifications



<span class="line"><!---->render pass is closed, but has the potential for future modifications<!----></span>



<br>





(for example to add a resolve attachment).  Under many circumstances, it



<span class="line"><!---->(for example to add a resolve attachment).  Under many circumstances, it<!----></span>



<br>





is expected that an open render pass cannot be in such a state.



<span class="line"><!---->is expected that an open render pass cannot be in such a state.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This assumption can be broken in this scenario:



<span class="line"><!---->This assumption can be broken in this scenario:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





- Open render pass, draw, etc



<span class="line"><!---->- Open render pass, draw, etc<!----></span>



<br>





- Change framebuffer binding



<span class="line"><!---->- Change framebuffer binding<!----></span>



<br>





- Change framebuffer binding back to original



<span class="line"><!---->- Change framebuffer binding back to original<!----></span>



<br>





- Masked Clear



<span class="line"><!---->- Masked Clear<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When ContextVk is synced before clear, it sees that the framebuffer



<span class="line"><!---->When ContextVk is synced before clear, it sees that the framebuffer<!----></span>



<br>





binding is changed (though it hasn't really), and it closes the render



<span class="line"><!---->binding is changed (though it hasn't really), and it closes the render<!----></span>



<br>





passes and sets the render pass dirty bit.  If a draw were to follow, a



<span class="line"><!---->passes and sets the render pass dirty bit.  If a draw were to follow, a<!----></span>



<br>





new render pass would have started (unnecessarily).  However, in the



<span class="line"><!---->new render pass would have started (unnecessarily).  However, in the<!----></span>



<br>





case of a masked clear, UtilsVk notices that the render pass is started,



<span class="line"><!---->case of a masked clear, UtilsVk notices that the render pass is started,<!----></span>



<br>





assumes it must be active, and continues recording to it.  While the



<span class="line"><!---->assumes it must be active, and continues recording to it.  While the<!----></span>



<br>





operation itself succeeds, the assumption that the render pass is active



<span class="line"><!---->operation itself succeeds, the assumption that the render pass is active<!----></span>



<br>





is false (and fails assertion).



<span class="line"><!---->is false (and fails assertion).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This change makes sure that framebuffer binding change is no-oped if the



<span class="line"><!---->This change makes sure that framebuffer binding change is no-oped if the<!----></span>



<br>





framebuffer is the same one that has opened the current render pass.  If



<span class="line"><!---->framebuffer is the same one that has opened the current render pass.  If<!----></span>



<br>





any application does unnecessary binding changes and back, it will be



<span class="line"><!---->any application does unnecessary binding changes and back, it will be<!----></span>



<br>





optimized by this change as well.



<span class="line"><!---->optimized by this change as well.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

M110: Vulkan: Don't close render pass if rebind to same fbo



<span class="line"><!---->M110: Vulkan: Don't close render pass if rebind to same fbo<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In the Vulkan backend, the render pass can occasionally (and



<span class="line"><!---->In the Vulkan backend, the render pass can occasionally (and<!----></span>



<br>





transiently) be in a state of "open but inactive".  This is when the



<span class="line"><!---->transiently) be in a state of "open but inactive".  This is when the<!----></span>



<br>





render pass is closed, but has the potential for future modifications



<span class="line"><!---->render pass is closed, but has the potential for future modifications<!----></span>



<br>





(for example to add a resolve attachment).  Under many circumstances, it



<span class="line"><!---->(for example to add a resolve attachment).  Under many circumstances, it<!----></span>



<br>





is expected that an open render pass cannot be in such a state.



<span class="line"><!---->is expected that an open render pass cannot be in such a state.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This assumption can be broken in this scenario:



<span class="line"><!---->This assumption can be broken in this scenario:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





- Open render pass, draw, etc



<span class="line"><!---->- Open render pass, draw, etc<!----></span>



<br>





- Change framebuffer binding



<span class="line"><!---->- Change framebuffer binding<!----></span>



<br>





- Change framebuffer binding back to original



<span class="line"><!---->- Change framebuffer binding back to original<!----></span>



<br>





- Masked Clear



<span class="line"><!---->- Masked Clear<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When ContextVk is synced before clear, it sees that the framebuffer



<span class="line"><!---->When ContextVk is synced before clear, it sees that the framebuffer<!----></span>



<br>





binding is changed (though it hasn't really), and it closes the render



<span class="line"><!---->binding is changed (though it hasn't really), and it closes the render<!----></span>



<br>





passes and sets the render pass dirty bit.  If a draw were to follow, a



<span class="line"><!---->passes and sets the render pass dirty bit.  If a draw were to follow, a<!----></span>



<br>





new render pass would have started (unnecessarily).  However, in the



<span class="line"><!---->new render pass would have started (unnecessarily).  However, in the<!----></span>



<br>





case of a masked clear, UtilsVk notices that the render pass is started,



<span class="line"><!---->case of a masked clear, UtilsVk notices that the render pass is started,<!----></span>



<br>





assumes it must be active, and continues recording to it.  While the



<span class="line"><!---->assumes it must be active, and continues recording to it.  While the<!----></span>



<br>





operation itself succeeds, the assumption that the render pass is active



<span class="line"><!---->operation itself succeeds, the assumption that the render pass is active<!----></span>



<br>





is false (and fails assertion).



<span class="line"><!---->is false (and fails assertion).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This change makes sure that framebuffer binding change is no-oped if the



<span class="line"><!---->This change makes sure that framebuffer binding change is no-oped if the<!----></span>



<br>





framebuffer is the same one that has opened the current render pass.  If



<span class="line"><!---->framebuffer is the same one that has opened the current render pass.  If<!----></span>



<br>





any application does unnecessary binding changes and back, it will be



<span class="line"><!---->any application does unnecessary binding changes and back, it will be<!----></span>



<br>





optimized by this change as well.



<span class="line"><!---->optimized by this change as well.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

M110: Vulkan: Don't close render pass if rebind to same fbo



<span class="line"><!---->M110: Vulkan: Don't close render pass if rebind to same fbo<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In the Vulkan backend, the render pass can occasionally (and



<span class="line"><!---->In the Vulkan backend, the render pass can occasionally (and<!----></span>



<br>





transiently) be in a state of "open but inactive".  This is when the



<span class="line"><!---->transiently) be in a state of "open but inactive".  This is when the<!----></span>



<br>





render pass is closed, but has the potential for future modifications



<span class="line"><!---->render pass is closed, but has the potential for future modifications<!----></span>



<br>





(for example to add a resolve attachment).  Under many circumstances, it



<span class="line"><!---->(for example to add a resolve attachment).  Under many circumstances, it<!----></span>



<br>





is expected that an open render pass cannot be in such a state.



<span class="line"><!---->is expected that an open render pass cannot be in such a state.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This assumption can be broken in this scenario:



<span class="line"><!---->This assumption can be broken in this scenario:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





- Open render pass, draw, etc



<span class="line"><!---->- Open render pass, draw, etc<!----></span>



<br>





- Change framebuffer binding



<span class="line"><!---->- Change framebuffer binding<!----></span>



<br>





- Change framebuffer binding back to original



<span class="line"><!---->- Change framebuffer binding back to original<!----></span>



<br>





- Masked Clear



<span class="line"><!---->- Masked Clear<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When ContextVk is synced before clear, it sees that the framebuffer



<span class="line"><!---->When ContextVk is synced before clear, it sees that the framebuffer<!----></span>



<br>





binding is changed (though it hasn't really), and it closes the render



<span class="line"><!---->binding is changed (though it hasn't really), and it closes the render<!----></span>



<br>





passes and sets the render pass dirty bit.  If a draw were to follow, a



<span class="line"><!---->passes and sets the render pass dirty bit.  If a draw were to follow, a<!----></span>



<br>





new render pass would have started (unnecessarily).  However, in the



<span class="line"><!---->new render pass would have started (unnecessarily).  However, in the<!----></span>



<br>





case of a masked clear, UtilsVk notices that the render pass is started,



<span class="line"><!---->case of a masked clear, UtilsVk notices that the render pass is started,<!----></span>



<br>





assumes it must be active, and continues recording to it.  While the



<span class="line"><!---->assumes it must be active, and continues recording to it.  While the<!----></span>



<br>





operation itself succeeds, the assumption that the render pass is active



<span class="line"><!---->operation itself succeeds, the assumption that the render pass is active<!----></span>



<br>





is false (and fails assertion).



<span class="line"><!---->is false (and fails assertion).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This change makes sure that framebuffer binding change is no-oped if the



<span class="line"><!---->This change makes sure that framebuffer binding change is no-oped if the<!----></span>



<br>





framebuffer is the same one that has opened the current render pass.  If



<span class="line"><!---->framebuffer is the same one that has opened the current render pass.  If<!----></span>



<br>





any application does unnecessary binding changes and back, it will be



<span class="line"><!---->any application does unnecessary binding changes and back, it will be<!----></span>



<br>





optimized by this change as well.



<span class="line"><!---->optimized by this change as well.<!----></span>



<br>

Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://chromium.googlesource.com/angle/angle/+/55e2b6daba9d6b10cb2ff97afcf08cece0a43754"><!---->https://chromium.googlesource.com/angle/angle/+/55e2b6daba9d6b10cb2ff97afcf08cece0a43754<!----></a>

<span class="line"><!---->commit <!----></span>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/55e2b6daba9d6b10cb2ff97afcf08cece0a43754"><!---->55e2b6daba9d6b10cb2ff97afcf08cece0a43754<!----></a>

Author: Shahbaz Youssefi <



<span class="line"><!---->Author: Shahbaz Youssefi &lt;<!----></span>





syoussefi@chromium.org



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="/u/syoussefi@chromium.org"><!---->syoussefi@chromium.org<!----></a>

Date: Fri Feb 17 04:16:46 2023



<span class="line"><!---->Date: Fri Feb 17 04:16:46 2023<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[M108-LTS] Vulkan: Don't close render pass if rebind to same fbo



<span class="line"><!---->[M108-LTS] Vulkan: Don't close render pass if rebind to same fbo<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





M108 merge issues:



<span class="line"><!---->M108 merge issues:<!----></span>



<br>





  src/libANGLE/renderer/vulkan/ContextVk.cpp:



<span class="line"><!---->  src/libANGLE/renderer/vulkan/ContextVk.cpp:<!----></span>



<br>





    - hasActiveRenderPass named hasStartedRenderPass in 108



<span class="line"><!---->    - hasActiveRenderPass named hasStartedRenderPass in 108<!----></span>



<br>





    - getLastRenderPassQueueSerial named getLastRenderPassSerial in 108



<span class="line"><!---->    - getLastRenderPassQueueSerial named getLastRenderPassSerial in 108<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In the Vulkan backend, the render pass can occasionally (and



<span class="line"><!---->In the Vulkan backend, the render pass can occasionally (and<!----></span>



<br>





transiently) be in a state of "open but inactive".  This is when the



<span class="line"><!---->transiently) be in a state of "open but inactive".  This is when the<!----></span>



<br>





render pass is closed, but has the potential for future modifications



<span class="line"><!---->render pass is closed, but has the potential for future modifications<!----></span>



<br>





(for example to add a resolve attachment).  Under many circumstances, it



<span class="line"><!---->(for example to add a resolve attachment).  Under many circumstances, it<!----></span>



<br>





is expected that an open render pass cannot be in such a state.



<span class="line"><!---->is expected that an open render pass cannot be in such a state.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This assumption can be broken in this scenario:



<span class="line"><!---->This assumption can be broken in this scenario:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





- Open render pass, draw, etc



<span class="line"><!---->- Open render pass, draw, etc<!----></span>



<br>





- Change framebuffer binding



<span class="line"><!---->- Change framebuffer binding<!----></span>



<br>





- Change framebuffer binding back to original



<span class="line"><!---->- Change framebuffer binding back to original<!----></span>



<br>





- Masked Clear



<span class="line"><!---->- Masked Clear<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When ContextVk is synced before clear, it sees that the framebuffer



<span class="line"><!---->When ContextVk is synced before clear, it sees that the framebuffer<!----></span>



<br>





binding is changed (though it hasn't really), and it closes the render



<span class="line"><!---->binding is changed (though it hasn't really), and it closes the render<!----></span>



<br>





passes and sets the render pass dirty bit.  If a draw were to follow, a



<span class="line"><!---->passes and sets the render pass dirty bit.  If a draw were to follow, a<!----></span>



<br>





new render pass would have started (unnecessarily).  However, in the



<span class="line"><!---->new render pass would have started (unnecessarily).  However, in the<!----></span>



<br>





case of a masked clear, UtilsVk notices that the render pass is started,

is false (and fails assertion).



<span class="line"><!---->is false (and fails assertion).<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->This change makes sure that framebuffer binding change is no-oped if the<!----></span>
